# Text Elements
Example 1.5 ^fT8JBccW

      consider the flow over two circular cylinders, one having 4 times the diameter 
of the other, as shown in Fig. the flow over the smaller cylinder has a freestream 
density, velocity and temperature as            and the bigger is given by 
we also have the relationship                    . Also assume that both   and a 
are proportional to the    , show the two cylinders are dynamically similar. ^wva2rykG

solution: we consider the Reynolds Number and the Mach Number
of the both flow ^n6bjBN8L

[[Important Variables and Numbers]] ^wQGxA0Ds

In the expression of these numbers, the ^ONfwS05y

and sound speed a ^GDxiAIHo

are still not defined. so we can consider how tp define it ^wuFc70cT

https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Temperature_dependence_of_viscosity ^YP9a6fiv

refer to the Hard sphere theory, we know that ^UpNA8cQb

and also  ^URt5t0nh

so we have:  ^GcsyTk2x

then we have that the temperature, velocity, density, pressure, etc. distributions are the same around two cylinders
shown in Fig below. ^26mIlijt

same curve
for flow 1 and 2 ^atcxmwJX

also,  the drag coefficients of two cylinders are the same, 
where  ^cJCKgX9Z

and  ^OX5JaRX5

also Note that the lift the cylinder is zero because of the
symmetrical about the horizontal axis ^xkohWHJU
